 WFI does not want to take any risk that would increase their injury

 is smartphone ko flipcart, samsung online store or samsung opera house se 27-28 sitambar ko kharid sakate hai
 After this it will also be found in offline retail stores
 Galaxy A7 main 6 inch kii phul echdi plus super amolade disple di gai he
 This smartphone runs on Samsung's in-house processor Octacore Exynos 7885
 disple aspect reshyo 18
 It is 5: 9 and has the protection of Gorilla Glass 3
 is divaais main Android 8
 0oreo based Samsung Experience user interface is given
 is smartphone main aapako fingerprint scinar najar nahin aayega, kyonki ise power batan ke saath said main rakhaa gaya he
 For photography, the triple camera module has been given in the rear of the Galaxy A7
 inamen se ek sensor 24 megapixl kaa jiskaa aparchar f / 1
 There is 7, the other is an 8 megapixel ultra wide sensor whose aperture f / 2
 4 he or teesraa depth sensor he jo 5 megapixl he

 front camera main live focus or pro liting mod kaa saport diya gaya he jiske tahat studio liting, filters or eaar imoji die gaye hai

 die gaye camere main seen optimizer feechar he jo artificial intelligence ko yuj karte hue khud se siniriyo detect karke camera settings ko aidjust karata he
 The Galaxy A7 has a 3,300 mah battery
 connactivity ke liye isamen wifai, bluetooth 5

 madhya pradesh main hue vidhansabha chunaav ke nattejey aa chuke hai
 There was a contest between Girish Gautam of Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) and Vidyavati Patel of Congress on the deitylab assembly seat
 yahaan bijepi pratyaashee girish gautam 45043 maton ke saath jeetne main kaamyaab hue
 Bahujan Samaj Party's Seema Sengar stood second
 unhen 43963 vot mili
 At the same time, Vidyavati Patel of Congress finished third
 unhen 30383 vot hasil hue

 bharat ne 26 july 1999 ko kargil yuddh (kargil War) main vijay hasil kii thi

 The Kargil war, also known as Operation Vijay, is the name of the armed conflict between India and Pakistan between May and July 1999 in Kargil district of Kashmir
 kargil yuddh (kargil War) lagbhag 60 dinon tak chalaa or 26 july ko uskaa ant hua
